Psalm 1

  1. (NIV) Blessed is the man who does not walk in the counsel of the wicked or stand in the way of sinners or sit in the seat of mockers.
  1. (KJV) Blessed is the man that walketh not in the counsel of the ungodly, nor standeth in the way of sinners, nor sitteth in the seat of the scornful.
  1. (NIV) But his delight is in the law of the LORD, and on his law he meditates day and night.
  1. (KJV) But his delight is in the law of the LORD; and in his law doth he meditate day and night.
  1. (NIV) He is like a tree planted by streams of water, which yields its fruit in season and whose leaf does not wither. Whatever he does prospers.
  1. (KJV) And he shall be like a tree planted by the rivers of water, that bringeth forth his fruit in his season; his leaf also shall not wither; and whatsoever he doeth shall prosper.
  1. (NIV) Not so the wicked! They are like chaff that the wind blows away.
  1. (KJV) The ungodly are not so: but are like the chaff which the wind driveth away.
  1. (NIV) Therefore the wicked will not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the assembly of the righteous.
  1. (KJV) Therefore the ungodly shall not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.
  1. (NIV) For the LORD watches over the way of the righteous, but the way of the wicked will perish.
  1. (KJV) For the LORD knoweth the way of the righteous: but the way of the ungodly shall perish.

Psalm 2

  1. (NIV) Why do the nations conspire [1] and the peoples plot in vain?
  1. (KJV) Why do the heathen rage, and the people imagine a vain thing?
  1. (NIV) The kings of the earth take their stand and the rulers gather together against the LORD and against his Anointed One. [2]
  1. (KJV) The kings of the earth set themselves, and the rulers take counsel together, against the LORD, and against his anointed, saying,
  1. (NIV) "Let us break their chains," they say, "and throw off their fetters."
  1. (KJV) Let us break their bands asunder, and cast away their cords from us.
  1. (NIV) The One enthroned in heaven laughs; the Lord scoffs at them.
  1. (KJV) He that sitteth in the heavens shall laugh: the Lord shall have them in derision.
  1. (NIV) Then he rebukes them in his anger and terrifies them in his wrath, saying,
  1. (KJV) Then shall he speak unto them in his wrath, and vex them in his sore displeasure.
  1. (NIV) "I have installed my King [3] on Zion, my holy hill."
  1. (KJV) Yet have I set my king upon my holy hill of Zion.
  1. (NIV) I will proclaim the decree of the LORD: He said to me, "You are my Son [4] ; today I have become your Father. [5]
  1. (KJV) I will declare the decree: the LORD hath said unto me, Thou art my Son; this day have I begotten thee.
  1. (NIV) Ask of me, and I will make the nations your inheritance, the ends of the earth your possession.
  1. (KJV) Ask of me, and I shall give thee the heathen for thine inheritance, and the uttermost parts of the earth for thy possession.
  1. (NIV) You will rule them with an iron scepter [6] ; you will dash them to pieces like pottery."
  1. (KJV) Thou shalt break them with a rod of iron; thou shalt dash them in pieces like a potter's vessel.
  1. (NIV) Therefore, you kings, be wise; be warned, you rulers of the earth.
  1. (KJV) Be wise now therefore, O ye kings: be instructed, ye judges of the earth.
  1. (NIV) Serve the LORD with fear and rejoice with trembling.
  1. (KJV) Serve the LORD with fear, and rejoice with trembling.
  1. (NIV) Kiss the Son, lest he be angry and you be destroyed in your way, for his wrath can flare up in a moment. Blessed are all who take refuge in him.
  1. (KJV) Kiss the Son, lest he be angry, and ye perish from the way, when his wrath is kindled but a little. Blessed are all they that put their trust in him.
  1. [1] Hebrew; Septuagint rage
  2. [2] Or anointed one
  3. [6] Or king
  4. [7] Or son; also in verse 12
  5. [7] Or have begotten you
  6. [9] Or will break them with a rod of iron

Psalm 3

A psalm of David. When he fled from his son Absalom.
  1. (NIV) O LORD, how many are my foes! How many rise up against me!
  1. (KJV) LORD, how are they increased that trouble me! many are they that rise up against me.
  1. (NIV) Many are saying of me, "God will not deliver him." Selah [1]
  1. (KJV) Many there be which say of my soul, There is no help for him in God. Selah.
  1. (NIV) But you are a shield around me, O LORD; you bestow glory on me and lift [2] up my head.
  1. (KJV) But thou, O LORD, art a shield for me; my glory, and the lifter up of mine head.
  1. (NIV) To the LORD I cry aloud, and he answers me from his holy hill. Selah
  1. (KJV) I cried unto the LORD with my voice, and he heard me out of his holy hill. Selah.
  1. (NIV) I lie down and sleep; I wake again, because the LORD sustains me.
  1. (KJV) I laid me down and slept; I awaked; for the LORD sustained me.
  1. (NIV) I will not fear the tens of thousands drawn up against me on every side.
  1. (KJV) I will not be afraid of ten thousands of people, that have set themselves against me round about.
  1. (NIV) Arise, O LORD! Deliver me, O my God! Strike all my enemies on the jaw; break the teeth of the wicked.
  1. (KJV) Arise, O LORD; save me, O my God: for thou hast smitten all mine enemies upon the cheek bone; thou hast broken the teeth of the ungodly.
  1. (NIV) From the LORD comes deliverance. May your blessing be on your people. Selah
  1. (KJV) Salvation belongeth unto the LORD: thy blessing is upon thy people. Selah.
  1. [2] A word of uncertain meaning, occurring frequently in the Psalms; possibly a musical term
  2. [3] Or LORD, my Glorious One, who lifts

Psalm 4

For the director of music. With stringed instruments. A psalm of David.
  1. (NIV) Answer me when I call to you, O my righteous God. Give me relief from my distress; be merciful to me and hear my prayer.
  1. (KJV) Hear me when I call, O God of my righteousness: thou hast enlarged me when I was in distress; have mercy upon me, and hear my prayer.
  1. (NIV) How long, O men, will you turn my glory into shame [1] ? How long will you love delusions and seek false gods [2] ? Selah
  1. (KJV) O ye sons of men, how long will ye turn my glory into shame? how long will ye love vanity, and seek after leasing? Selah.
  1. (NIV) Know that the LORD has set apart the godly for himself; the LORD will hear when I call to him.
  1. (KJV) But know that the LORD hath set apart him that is godly for himself: the LORD will hear when I call unto him.
  1. (NIV) In your anger do not sin; when you are on your beds, search your hearts and be silent. Selah
  1. (KJV) Stand in awe, and sin not: commune with your own heart upon your bed, and be still. Selah.
  1. (NIV) Offer right sacrifices and trust in the LORD.
  1. (KJV) Offer the sacrifices of righteousness, and put your trust in the LORD.
  1. (NIV) Many are asking, "Who can show us any good?" Let the light of your face shine upon us, O LORD.
  1. (KJV) There be many that say, Who will shew us any good? LORD, lift thou up the light of thy countenance upon us.
  1. (NIV) You have filled my heart with greater joy than when their grain and new wine abound.
  1. (KJV) Thou hast put gladness in my heart, more than in the time that their corn and their wine increased.
  1. (NIV) I will lie down and sleep in peace, for you alone, O LORD, make me dwell in safety.
  1. (KJV) I will both lay me down in peace, and sleep: for thou, LORD, only makest me dwell in safety.
  1. [2] Or you dishonor my Glorious One
  2. [2] Or seek lies

Psalm 5

For the director of music. For flutes. A psalm of David.
  1. (NIV) Give ear to my words, O LORD, consider my sighing.
  1. (KJV) Give ear to my words, O LORD, consider my meditation.
  1. (NIV) Listen to my cry for help, my King and my God, for to you I pray.
  1. (KJV) Hearken unto the voice of my cry, my King, and my God: for unto thee will I pray.
  1. (NIV) In the morning, O LORD, you hear my voice; in the morning I lay my requests before you and wait in expectation.
  1. (KJV) My voice shalt thou hear in the morning, O LORD; in the morning will I direct my prayer unto thee, and will look up.
  1. (NIV) You are not a God who takes pleasure in evil; with you the wicked cannot dwell.
  1. (KJV) For thou art not a God that hath pleasure in wickedness: neither shall evil dwell with thee.
  1. (NIV) The arrogant cannot stand in your presence; you hate all who do wrong.
  1. (KJV) The foolish shall not stand in thy sight: thou hatest all workers of iniquity.
  1. (NIV) You destroy those who tell lies; bloodthirsty and deceitful men the LORD abhors.
  1. (KJV) Thou shalt destroy them that speak leasing: the LORD will abhor the bloody and deceitful man.
  1. (NIV) But I, by your great mercy, will come into your house; in reverence will I bow down toward your holy temple.
  1. (KJV) But as for me, I will come into thy house in the multitude of thy mercy: and in thy fear will I worship toward thy holy temple.
  1. (NIV) Lead me, O LORD, in your righteousness because of my enemies-- make straight your way before me.
  1. (KJV) Lead me, O LORD, in thy righteousness because of mine enemies; make thy way straight before my face.
  1. (NIV) Not a word from their mouth can be trusted; their heart is filled with destruction. Their throat is an open grave; with their tongue they speak deceit.
  1. (KJV) For there is no faithfulness in their mouth; their inward part is very wickedness; their throat is an open sepulchre; they flatter with their tongue.
  1. (NIV) Declare them guilty, O God! Let their intrigues be their downfall. Banish them for their many sins, for they have rebelled against you.
  1. (KJV) Destroy thou them, O God; let them fall by their own counsels; cast them out in the multitude of their transgressions; for they have rebelled against thee.
  1. (NIV) But let all who take refuge in you be glad; let them ever sing for joy. Spread your protection over them, that those who love your name may rejoice in you.
  1. (KJV) But let all those that put their trust in thee rejoice: let them ever shout for joy, because thou defendest them: let them also that love thy name be joyful in thee.
  1. (NIV) For surely, O LORD, you bless the righteous; you surround them with your favor as with a shield.
  1. (KJV) For thou, LORD, wilt bless the righteous; with favour wilt thou compass him as with a shield.

Psalm 6

For the director of music. With stringed instruments. According to sheminith. [1] A psalm of David.
  1. (NIV) O LORD, do not rebuke me in your anger or discipline me in your wrath.
  1. (KJV) O LORD, rebuke me not in thine anger, neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.
  1. (NIV) Be merciful to me, LORD, for I am faint; O LORD, heal me, for my bones are in agony.
  1. (KJV) Have mercy upon me, O LORD; for I am weak: O LORD, heal me; for my bones are vexed.
  1. (NIV) My soul is in anguish. How long, O LORD, how long?
  1. (KJV) My soul is also sore vexed: but thou, O LORD, how long?
  1. (NIV) Turn, O LORD, and deliver me; save me because of your unfailing love.
  1. (KJV) Return, O LORD, deliver my soul: oh save me for thy mercies' sake.
  1. (NIV) No one remembers you when he is dead. Who praises you from the grave [2] ?
  1. (KJV) For in death there is no remembrance of thee: in the grave who shall give thee thanks?
  1. (NIV) I am worn out from groaning; all night long I flood my bed with weeping and drench my couch with tears.
  1. (KJV) I am weary with my groaning; all the night make I my bed to swim; I water my couch with my tears.
  1. (NIV) My eyes grow weak with sorrow; they fail because of all my foes.
  1. (KJV) Mine eye is consumed because of grief; it waxeth old because of all mine enemies.
  1. (NIV) Away from me, all you who do evil, for the LORD has heard my weeping.
  1. (KJV) Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; for the LORD hath heard the voice of my weeping.
  1. (NIV) The LORD has heard my cry for mercy; the LORD accepts my prayer.
  1. (KJV) The LORD hath heard my supplication; the LORD will receive my prayer.
  1. (NIV) All my enemies will be ashamed and dismayed; they will turn back in sudden disgrace.
  1. (KJV) Let all mine enemies be ashamed and sore vexed: let them return and be ashamed suddenly.
  1. [Title] Probably a musical term
  2. [5] Hebrew Sheol

Psalm 7

A shiggaion [1] of David, which he sang to the LORD concerning Cush, a Benjamite.
  1. (NIV) O LORD my God, I take refuge in you; save and deliver me from all who pursue me,
  1. (KJV) O Lord my God, in thee do I put my trust: save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me:
  1. (NIV) or they will tear me like a lion and rip me to pieces with no one to rescue me.
  1. (KJV) Lest he tear my soul like a lion, rending it in pieces, while there is none to deliver.
  1. (NIV) O LORD my God, if I have done this and there is guilt on my hands--
  1. (KJV) O LORD my God, if I have done this; if there be iniquity in my hands;
  1. (NIV) if I have done evil to him who is at peace with me or without cause have robbed my foe--
  1. (KJV) If I have rewarded evil unto him that was at peace with me; (yea, I have delivered him that without cause is mine enemy:)
  1. (NIV) then let my enemy pursue and overtake me; let him trample my life to the ground and make me sleep in the dust. Selah
  1. (KJV) Let the enemy persecute my soul, and take it; yea, let him tread down my life upon the earth, and lay mine honour in the dust. Selah.
  1. (NIV) Arise, O LORD, in your anger; rise up against the rage of my enemies. Awake, my God; decree justice.
  1. (KJV) Arise, O LORD, in thine anger, lift up thyself because of the rage of mine enemies: and awake for me to the judgment that thou hast commanded.
  1. (NIV) Let the assembled peoples gather around you. Rule over them from on high;
  1. (KJV) So shall the congregation of the people compass thee about: for their sakes therefore return thou on high.
  1. (NIV) let the LORD judge the peoples. Judge me, O LORD, according to my righteousness, according to my integrity, O Most High.
  1. (KJV) The LORD shall judge the people: judge me, O LORD, according to my righteousness, and according to mine integrity that is in me.
  1. (NIV) O righteous God, who searches minds and hearts, bring to an end the violence of the wicked and make the righteous secure.
  1. (KJV) Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end; but establish the just: for the righteous God trieth the hearts and reins.
  1. (NIV) My shield [2] is God Most High, who saves the upright in heart.
  1. (KJV) My defence is of God, which saveth the upright in heart.
  1. (NIV) God is a righteous judge, a God who expresses his wrath every day.
  1. (KJV) God judgeth the righteous, and God is angry with the wicked every day.
  1. (NIV) If he does not relent, he [3] will sharpen his sword; he will bend and string his bow.
  1. (KJV) If he turn not, he will whet his sword; he hath bent his bow, and made it ready.
  1. (NIV) He has prepared his deadly weapons; he makes ready his flaming arrows.
  1. (KJV) He hath also prepared for him the instruments of death; he ordaineth his arrows against the persecutors.
  1. (NIV) He who is pregnant with evil and conceives trouble gives birth to disillusionment.
  1. (KJV) Behold, he travaileth with iniquity, and hath conceived mischief, and brought forth falsehood.
  1. (NIV) He who digs a hole and scoops it out falls into the pit he has made.
  1. (KJV) He made a pit, and digged it, and is fallen into the ditch which he made.
  1. (NIV) The trouble he causes recoils on himself; his violence comes down on his own head.
  1. (KJV) His mischief shall return upon his own head, and his violent dealing shall come down upon his own pate.
  1. (NIV) I will give thanks to the LORD because of his righteousness and will sing praise to the name of the LORD Most High.
  1. (KJV) I will praise the LORD according to his righteousness: and will sing praise to the name of the LORD most high.
  1. [Title] Probably a literary or musical term
  2. [10] Or sovereign
  3. [12] Or If a man does not repent, God

Psalm 8

For the director of music. According to gittith. [1] A psalm of David.
  1. (NIV) O LORD, our Lord, how majestic is your name in all the earth! You have set your glory above the heavens.
  1. (KJV) O LORD our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the earth! who hast set thy glory above the heavens.
  1. (NIV) From the lips of children and infants you have ordained praise [2] because of your enemies, to silence the foe and the avenger.
  1. (KJV) Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings hast thou ordained strength because of thine enemies, that thou mightest still the enemy and the avenger.
  1. (NIV) When I consider your heavens, the work of your fingers, the moon and the stars, which you have set in place,
  1. (KJV) When I consider thy heavens, the work of thy fingers, the moon and the stars, which thou hast ordained;
  1. (NIV) what is man that you are mindful of him, the son of man that you care for him?
  1. (KJV) What is man, that thou art mindful of him? and the son of man, that thou visitest him?
  1. (NIV) You made him a little lower than the heavenly beings [3] and crowned him with glory and honor.
  1. (KJV) For thou hast made him a little lower than the angels, and hast crowned him with glory and honour.
  1. (NIV) You made him ruler over the works of your hands; you put everything under his feet:
  1. (KJV) Thou madest him to have dominion over the works of thy hands; thou hast put all things under his feet:
  1. (NIV) all flocks and herds, and the beasts of the field,
  1. (KJV) All sheep and oxen, yea, and the beasts of the field;
  1. (NIV) the birds of the air, and the fish of the sea, all that swim the paths of the seas.
  1. (KJV) The fowl of the air, and the fish of the sea, and whatsoever passeth through the paths of the seas.
  1. (NIV) O LORD, our Lord, how majestic is your name in all the earth!
  1. (KJV) O LORD our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the earth!
  1. [Title] Probably a musical term
  2. [2] Or strength
  3. [5] Or than God

Psalm 9

For the director of music. To [the tune of] "The Death of the Son." A psalm of David. [1]
  1. (NIV) I will praise you, O LORD, with all my heart; I will tell of all your wonders.
  1. (KJV) I will praise thee, O LORD, with my whole heart; I will shew forth all thy marvellous works.
  1. (NIV) I will be glad and rejoice in you; I will sing praise to your name, O Most High.
  1. (KJV) I will be glad and rejoice in thee: I will sing praise to thy name, O thou most High.
  1. (NIV) My enemies turn back; they stumble and perish before you.
  1. (KJV) When mine enemies are turned back, they shall fall and perish at thy presence.
  1. (NIV) For you have upheld my right and my cause; you have sat on your throne, judging righteously.
  1. (KJV) For thou hast maintained my right and my cause; thou satest in the throne judging right.
  1. (NIV) You have rebuked the nations and destroyed the wicked; you have blotted out their name for ever and ever.
  1. (KJV) Thou hast rebuked the heathen, thou hast destroyed the wicked, thou hast put out their name for ever and ever.
  1. (NIV) Endless ruin has overtaken the enemy, you have uprooted their cities; even the memory of them has perished.
  1. (KJV) O thou enemy, destructions are come to a perpetual end: and thou hast destroyed cities; their memorial is perished with them.
  1. (NIV) The LORD reigns forever; he has established his throne for judgment.
  1. (KJV) But the LORD shall endure for ever: he hath prepared his throne for judgment.
  1. (NIV) He will judge the world in righteousness; he will govern the peoples with justice.
  1. (KJV) And he shall judge the world in righteousness, he shall minister judgment to the people in uprightness.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is a refuge for the oppressed, a stronghold in times of trouble.
  1. (KJV) The LORD also will be a refuge for the oppressed, a refuge in times of trouble.
  1. (NIV) Those who know your name will trust in you, for you, LORD, have never forsaken those who seek you.
  1. (KJV) And they that know thy name will put their trust in thee: for thou, LORD, hast not forsaken them that seek thee.
  1. (NIV) Sing praises to the LORD, enthroned in Zion; proclaim among the nations what he has done.
  1. (KJV) Sing praises to the LORD, which dwelleth in Zion: declare among the people his doings.
  1. (NIV) For he who avenges blood remembers; he does not ignore the cry of the afflicted.
  1. (KJV) When he maketh inquisition for blood, he remembereth them: he forgetteth not the cry of the humble.
  1. (NIV) O LORD, see how my enemies persecute me! Have mercy and lift me up from the gates of death,
  1. (KJV) Have mercy upon me, O LORD; consider my trouble which I suffer of them that hate me, thou that liftest me up from the gates of death:
  1. (NIV) that I may declare your praises in the gates of the Daughter of Zion and there rejoice in your salvation.
  1. (KJV) That I may shew forth all thy praise in the gates of the daughter of Zion: I will rejoice in thy salvation.
  1. (NIV) The nations have fallen into the pit they have dug; their feet are caught in the net they have hidden.
  1. (KJV) The heathen are sunk down in the pit that they made: in the net which they hid is their own foot taken.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is known by his justice; the wicked are ensnared by the work of their hands. Higgaion. [2] Selah
  1. (KJV) The LORD is known by the judgment which he executeth: the wicked is snared in the work of his own hands. Higgaion. Selah.
  1. (NIV) The wicked return to the grave, [3] all the nations that forget God.
  1. (KJV) The wicked shall be turned into hell, and all the nations that forget God.
  1. (NIV) But the needy will not always be forgotten, nor the hope of the afflicted ever perish.
  1. (KJV) For the needy shall not alway be forgotten: the expectation of the poor shall not perish for ever.
  1. (NIV) Arise, O LORD, let not man triumph; let the nations be judged in your presence.
  1. (KJV) Arise, O LORD; let not man prevail: let the heathen be judged in thy sight.
  1. (NIV) Strike them with terror, O LORD; let the nations know they are but men. Selah
  1. (KJV) Put them in fear, O LORD: that the nations may know themselves to be but men. Selah.
  1. [Title] Psalms 9 and 10 may have been originally a single acrostic poem, the stanzas of which begin with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet. In the Septuagint they constitute one psalm.
  2. [16] Or Meditation; possibly a musical notation
  3. [17] Hebrew Sheol

Psalm 10

[1]
  1. (NIV) Why, O LORD, do you stand far off? Why do you hide yourself in times of trouble?
  1. (KJV) Why standest thou afar off, O LORD? why hidest thou thyself in times of trouble?
  1. (NIV) In his arrogance the wicked man hunts down the weak, who are caught in the schemes he devises.
  1. (KJV) The wicked in his pride doth persecute the poor: let them be taken in the devices that they have imagined.
  1. (NIV) He boasts of the cravings of his heart; he blesses the greedy and reviles the LORD.
  1. (KJV) For the wicked boasteth of his heart's desire, and blesseth the covetous, whom the LORD abhorreth.
  1. (NIV) In his pride the wicked does not seek him; in all his thoughts there is no room for God.
  1. (KJV) The wicked, through the pride of his countenance, will not seek after God: God is not in all his thoughts.
  1. (NIV) His ways are always prosperous; he is haughty and your laws are far from him; he sneers at all his enemies.
  1. (KJV) His ways are always grievous; thy judgments are far above out of his sight: as for all his enemies, he puffeth at them.
  1. (NIV) He says to himself, "Nothing will shake me; I'll always be happy and never have trouble."
  1. (KJV) He hath said in his heart, I shall not be moved: for I shall never be in adversity.
  1. (NIV) His mouth is full of curses and lies and threats; trouble and evil are under his tongue.
  1. (KJV) His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and fraud: under his tongue is mischief and vanity.
  1. (NIV) He lies in wait near the villages; from ambush he murders the innocent, watching in secret for his victims.
  1. (KJV) He sitteth in the lurking places of the villages: in the secret places doth he murder the innocent: his eyes are privily set against the poor.
  1. (NIV) He lies in wait like a lion in cover; he lies in wait to catch the helpless; he catches the helpless and drags them off in his net.
  1. (KJV) He lieth in wait secretly as a lion in his den: he lieth in wait to catch the poor: he doth catch the poor, when he draweth him into his net.
  1. (NIV) His victims are crushed, they collapse; they fall under his strength.
  1. (KJV) He croucheth, and humbleth himself, that the poor may fall by his strong ones.
  1. (NIV) He says to himself, "God has forgotten; he covers his face and never sees."
  1. (KJV) He hath said in his heart, God hath forgotten: he hideth his face; he will never see it.
  1. (NIV) Arise, LORD! Lift up your hand, O God. Do not forget the helpless.
  1. (KJV) Arise, O LORD; O God, lift up thine hand: forget not the humble.
  1. (NIV) Why does the wicked man revile God? Why does he say to himself, "He won't call me to account"?
  1. (KJV) Wherefore doth the wicked contemn God? he hath said in his heart, Thou wilt not require it.
  1. (NIV) But you, O God, do see trouble and grief; you consider it to take it in hand. The victim commits himself to you; you are the helper of the fatherless.
  1. (KJV) Thou hast seen it; for thou beholdest mischief and spite, to requite it with thy hand: the poor committeth himself unto thee; thou art the helper of the fatherless.
  1. (NIV) Break the arm of the wicked and evil man; call him to account for his wickedness that would not be found out.
  1. (KJV) Break thou the arm of the wicked and the evil man: seek out his wickedness till thou find none.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is King for ever and ever; the nations will perish from his land.
  1. (KJV) The LORD is King for ever and ever: the heathen are perished out of his land.

For the director of music. Of David the servant of the LORD. He sang to the LORD the words of this song when the LORD delivered him from the hand of all his enemies and from the hand of Saul. He said:

  1. (KJV) I will love thee, O LORD, my strength.

  1. (KJV) In my distress I called upon the LORD, and cried unto my God: he heard my voice out of his temple, and my cry came before him, even into his ears.

  1. (KJV) He sent from above, he took me, he drew me out of many waters.

  1. (KJV) He brought me forth also into a large place; he delivered me, because he delighted in me.
  1. (NIV) The LORD has dealt with me according to my righteousness; according to the cleanness of my hands he has rewarded me.
  1. (KJV) The LORD rewarded me according to my righteousness; according to the cleanness of my hands hath he recompensed me.

Psalm 27

Of David.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is my light and my salvation-- whom shall I fear? The LORD is the stronghold of my life-- of whom shall I be afraid?
  1. (KJV) The LORD is my light and my salvation; whom shall I fear? the LORD is the strength of my life; of whom shall I be afraid?
  1. (NIV) When evil men advance against me to devour my flesh, [1] when my enemies and my foes attack me, they will stumble and fall.
  1. (KJV) When the wicked, even mine enemies and my foes, came upon me to eat up my flesh, they stumbled and fell.
  1. (NIV) Though an army besiege me, my heart will not fear; though war break out against me, even then will I be confident.
  1. (KJV) Though an host should encamp against me, my heart shall not fear: though war should rise against me, in this will I be confident.
  1. (NIV) One thing I ask of the LORD, this is what I seek: that I may dwell in the house of the LORD all the days of my life, to gaze upon the beauty of the LORD and to seek him in his temple.
  1. (KJV) One thing have I desired of the LORD, that will I seek after; that I may dwell in the house of the LORD all the days of my life, to behold the beauty of the LORD, and to inquire in his temple.
  1. (NIV) For in the day of trouble he will keep me safe in his dwelling; he will hide me in the shelter of his tabernacle and set me high upon a rock.
  1. (KJV) For in the time of trouble he shall hide me in his pavilion: in the secret of his tabernacle shall he hide me; he shall set me up upon a rock.
  1. (NIV) Then my head will be exalted above the enemies who surround me; at his tabernacle will I sacrifice with shouts of joy; I will sing and make music to the LORD.
  1. (KJV) And now shall mine head be lifted up above mine enemies round about me: therefore will I offer in his tabernacle sacrifices of joy; I will sing, yea, I will sing praises unto the LORD.
  1. (NIV) Hear my voice when I call, O LORD; be merciful to me and answer me.
  1. (KJV) Hear, O LORD, when I cry with my voice: have mercy also upon me, and answer me.
  1. (NIV) My heart says of you, "Seek his [2] face!" Your face, LORD, I will seek.
  1. (KJV) When thou saidst, Seek ye my face; my heart said unto thee, Thy face, LORD, will I seek.
  1. (NIV) Do not hide your face from me, do not turn your servant away in anger; you have been my helper. Do not reject me or forsake me, O God my Savior.
  1. (KJV) Hide not thy face far from me; put not thy servant away in anger: thou hast been my help; leave me not, neither forsake me, O God of my salvation.
  1. (NIV) Though my father and mother forsake me, the LORD will receive me.
  1. (KJV) When my father and my mother forsake me, then the LORD will take me up.
  1. (NIV) Teach me your way, O LORD; lead me in a straight path because of my oppressors.

Psalm 35

Of David.
  1. (NIV) Contend, O LORD, with those who contend with me; fight against those who fight against me.

Psalm 38

A psalm of David. A petition.
  1. (NIV) O LORD, do not rebuke me in your anger or discipline me in your wrath.
  1. (KJV) O LORD, rebuke me not in thy wrath: neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.
  1. (NIV) For your arrows have pierced me, and your hand has come down upon me.
  1. (KJV) For thine arrows stick fast in me, and thy hand presseth me sore.
  1. (NIV) Because of your wrath there is no health in my body; my bones have no soundness because of my sin.
  1. (KJV) There is no soundness in my flesh because of thine anger; neither is there any rest in my bones because of my sin.
  1. (NIV) My guilt has overwhelmed me like a burden too heavy to bear.
  1. (KJV) For mine iniquities are gone over mine head: as an heavy burden they are too heavy for me.
  1. (NIV) My wounds fester and are loathsome because of my sinful folly.
  1. (KJV) My wounds stink and are corrupt because of my foolishness.
  1. (NIV) I am bowed down and brought very low; all day long I go about mourning.
  1. (KJV) I am troubled; I am bowed down greatly; I go mourning all the day long.
  1. (NIV) My back is filled with searing pain; there is no health in my body.
  1. (KJV) For my loins are filled with a loathsome disease: and there is no soundness in my flesh.
  1. (NIV) I am feeble and utterly crushed; I groan in anguish of heart.
  1. (KJV) I am feeble and sore broken: I have roared by reason of the disquietness of my heart.
  1. (NIV) All my longings lie open before you, O Lord; my sighing is not hidden from you.
  1. (KJV) Lord, all my desire is before thee; and my groaning is not hid from thee.
  1. (NIV) My heart pounds, my strength fails me; even the light has gone from my eyes.
  1. (KJV) My heart panteth, my strength faileth me: as for the light of mine eyes, it also is gone from me.
  1. (NIV) My friends and companions avoid me because of my wounds; my neighbors stay far away.
  1. (KJV) My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my sore; and my kinsmen stand afar off.
  1. (NIV) Those who seek my life set their traps, those who would harm me talk of my ruin; all day long they plot deception.
  1. (KJV) They also that seek after my life lay snares for me: and they that seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and imagine deceits all the day long.
  1. (NIV) I am like a deaf man, who cannot hear, like a mute, who cannot open his mouth;
  1. (KJV) But I, as a deaf man, heard not; and I was as a dumb man that openeth not his mouth.
  1. (NIV) I have become like a man who does not hear, whose mouth can offer no reply.
  1. (KJV) Thus I was as a man that heareth not, and in whose mouth are no reproofs.
  1. (NIV) I wait for you, O LORD; you will answer, O Lord my God.
  1. (KJV) For in thee, O LORD, do I hope: thou wilt hear, O Lord my God.
  1. (NIV) For I said, "Do not let them gloat or exalt themselves over me when my foot slips."
  1. (KJV) For I said, Hear me, lest otherwise they should rejoice over me: when my foot slippeth, they magnify themselves against me.
  1. (NIV) For I am about to fall, and my pain is ever with me.
  1. (KJV) For I am ready to halt, and my sorrow is continually before me.
  1. (NIV) I confess my iniquity; I am troubled by my sin.
  1. (KJV) For I will declare mine iniquity; I will be sorry for my sin.
  1. (NIV) Many are those who are my vigorous enemies; those who hate me without reason are numerous.
  1. (KJV) But mine enemies are lively, and they are strong: and they that hate me wrongfully are multiplied.
  1. (NIV) Those who repay my good with evil slander me when I pursue what is good.
  1. (KJV) They also that render evil for good are mine adversaries; because I follow the thing that good is.
  1. (NIV) O LORD, do not forsake me; be not far from me, O my God.
  1. (KJV) Forsake me not, O LORD: O my God, be not far from me.
  1. (NIV) Come quickly to help me, O Lord my Savior.
  1. (KJV) Make haste to help me, O Lord my salvation.

Psalm 67

For the director of music. With stringed instruments. A psalm. A song.
  1. (NIV) May God be gracious to us and bless us and make his face shine upon us, Selah
  1. (KJV) God be merciful unto us, and bless us; and cause his face to shine upon us; Selah.
  1. (NIV) that your ways may be known on earth, your salvation among all nations.
  1. (KJV) That thy way may be known upon earth, thy saving health among all nations.
  1. (NIV) May the peoples praise you, O God; may all the peoples praise you.
  1. (KJV) Let the people praise thee, O God; let all the people praise thee.
  1. (NIV) May the nations be glad and sing for joy, for you rule the peoples justly and guide the nations of the earth. Selah
  1. (KJV) O let the nations be glad and sing for joy: for thou shalt judge the people righteously, and govern the nations upon earth. Selah.
  1. (NIV) May the peoples praise you, O God; may all the peoples praise you.
  1. (KJV) Let the people praise thee, O God; let all the people praise thee.
  1. (NIV) Then the land will yield its harvest, and God, our God, will bless us.
  1. (KJV) Then shall the earth yield her increase; and God, even our own God, shall bless us.
  1. (NIV) God will bless us, and all the ends of the earth will fear him.
  1. (KJV) God shall bless us; and all the ends of the earth shall fear him.

Psalm 68

For the director of music. Of David. A psalm. A song.
  1. (NIV) May God arise, may his enemies be scattered; may his foes flee before him.
  1. (KJV) Let God arise, let his enemies be scattered: let them also that hate him flee before him.
  1. (NIV) As smoke is blown away by the wind, may you blow them away; as wax melts before the fire, may the wicked perish before God.
  1. (KJV) As smoke is driven away, so drive them away: as wax melteth before the fire, so let the wicked perish at the presence of God.
  1. (NIV) But may the righteous be glad and rejoice before God; may they be happy and joyful.
  1. (KJV) But let the righteous be glad; let them rejoice before God: yea, let them exceedingly rejoice.
  1. (NIV) Sing to God, sing praise to his name, extol him who rides on the clouds [1] -- his name is the LORD-- and rejoice before him.
  1. (KJV) Sing unto God, sing praises to his name: extol him that rideth upon the heavens by his name JAH, and rejoice before him.
  1. (NIV) A father to the fatherless, a defender of widows, is God in his holy dwelling.
  1. (KJV) A father of the fatherless, and a judge of the widows, is God in his holy habitation.
  1. (NIV) God sets the lonely in families, [2] he leads forth the prisoners with singing; but the rebellious live in a sun-scorched land.
  1. (KJV) God setteth the solitary in families: he bringeth out those which are bound with chains: but the rebellious dwell in a dry land.
  1. (NIV) When you went out before your people, O God, when you marched through the wasteland, Selah
  1. (KJV) O God, when thou wentest forth before thy people, when thou didst march through the wilderness; Selah:
  1. (NIV) the earth shook, the heavens poured down rain, before God, the One of Sinai, before God, the God of Israel.
  1. (KJV) The earth shook, the heavens also dropped at the presence of God: even Sinai itself was moved at the presence of God, the God of Israel.
  1. (NIV) You gave abundant showers, O God; you refreshed your weary inheritance.
  1. (KJV) Thou, O God, didst send a plentiful rain, whereby thou didst confirm thine inheritance, when it was weary.
  1. (NIV) Your people settled in it, and from your bounty, O God, you provided for the poor.
  1. (KJV) Thy congregation hath dwelt therein: thou, O God, hast prepared of thy goodness for the poor.
  1. (NIV) The Lord announced the word, and great was the company of those who proclaimed it:
  1. (KJV) The Lord gave the word: great was the company of those that published it.
  1. (NIV) "Kings and armies flee in haste; in the camps men divide the plunder.
  1. (KJV) Kings of armies did flee apace: and she that tarried at home divided the spoil.
  1. (NIV) Even while you sleep among the campfires, [3] the wings of [my] dove are sheathed with silver, its feathers with shining gold."
  1. (KJV) Though ye have lien among the pots, yet shall ye be as the wings of a dove covered with silver, and her feathers with yellow gold.
  1. (NIV) When the Almighty [4] scattered the kings in the land, it was like snow fallen on Zalmon.
  1. (KJV) When the Almighty scattered kings in it, it was white as snow in Salmon.
  1. (NIV) The mountains of Bashan are majestic mountains; rugged are the mountains of Bashan.
  1. (KJV) The hill of God is as the hill of Bashan; an high hill as the hill of Bashan.
  1. (NIV) Why gaze in envy, O rugged mountains, at the mountain where God chooses to reign, where the LORD himself will dwell forever?
  1. (KJV) Why leap ye, ye high hills? this is the hill which God desireth to dwell in; yea, the LORD will dwell in it for ever.
  1. (NIV) The chariots of God are tens of thousands and thousands of thousands; the Lord [has come] from Sinai into his sanctuary.
  1. (KJV) The chariots of God are twenty thousand, even thousands of angels: the Lord is among them, as in Sinai, in the holy place.
  1. (NIV) When you ascended on high, you led captives in your train; you received gifts from men, even from [5] the rebellious-- that you, [6] O LORD God, might dwell there.
  1. (KJV) Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast led captivity captive: thou hast received gifts for men; yea, for the rebellious also, that the LORD God might dwell among them.
  1. (NIV) Praise be to the Lord, to God our Savior, who daily bears our burdens. Selah
  1. (KJV) Blessed be the Lord, who daily loadeth us with benefits, even the God of our salvation. Selah.
  1. (NIV) Our God is a God who saves; from the Sovereign LORD comes escape from death.
  1. (KJV) He that is our God is the God of salvation; and unto God the Lord belong the issues from death.
  1. (NIV) Surely God will crush the heads of his enemies, the hairy crowns of those who go on in their sins.
  1. (KJV) But God shall wound the head of his enemies, and the hairy scalp of such an one as goeth on still in his trespasses.
  1. (NIV) The Lord says, "I will bring them from Bashan; I will bring them from the depths of the sea,
  1. (KJV) The Lord said, I will bring again from Bashan, I will bring my people again from the depths of the sea:
  1. (NIV) that you may plunge your feet in the blood of your foes, while the tongues of your dogs have their share."
  1. (KJV) That thy foot may be dipped in the blood of thine enemies, and the tongue of thy dogs in the same.
  1. (NIV) Your procession has come into view, O God, the procession of my God and King into the sanctuary.
  1. (KJV) They have seen thy goings, O God; even the goings of my God, my King, in the sanctuary.
  1. (NIV) In front are the singers, after them the musicians; with them are the maidens playing tambourines.
  1. (KJV) The singers went before, the players on instruments followed after; among them were the damsels playing with timbrels.
  1. (NIV) Praise God in the great congregation; praise the LORD in the assembly of Israel.
  1. (KJV) Bless ye God in the congregations, even the Lord, from the fountain of Israel.
  1. (NIV) There is the little tribe of Benjamin, leading them, there the great throng of Judah's princes, and there the princes of Zebulun and of Naphtali.
  1. (KJV) There is little Benjamin with their ruler, the princes of Judah and their council, the princes of Zebulun, and the princes of Naphtali.
  1. (NIV) Summon your power, O God [7] ; show us your strength, O God, as you have done before.
  1. (KJV) Thy God hath commanded thy strength: strengthen, O God, that which thou hast wrought for us.
  1. (NIV) Because of your temple at Jerusalem kings will bring you gifts.
  1. (KJV) Because of thy temple at Jerusalem shall kings bring presents unto thee.
  1. (NIV) Rebuke the beast among the reeds, the herd of bulls among the calves of the nations. Humbled, may it bring bars of silver. Scatter the nations who delight in war.
  1. (KJV) Rebuke the company of spearmen, the multitude of the bulls, with the calves of the people, till every one submit himself with pieces of silver: scatter thou the people that delight in war.
  1. (NIV) Envoys will come from Egypt; Cush [8] will submit herself to God.
  1. (KJV) Princes shall come out of Egypt; Ethiopia shall soon stretch out her hands unto God.
  1. (NIV) Sing to God, O kingdoms of the earth, sing praise to the Lord, Selah
  1. (KJV) Sing unto God, ye kingdoms of the earth; O sing praises unto the Lord; Selah:
  1. (NIV) to him who rides the ancient skies above, who thunders with mighty voice.
  1. (KJV) To him that rideth upon the heavens of heavens, which were of old; lo, he doth send out his voice, and that a mighty voice.
  1. (NIV) Proclaim the power of God, whose majesty is over Israel, whose power is in the skies.
  1. (KJV) Ascribe ye strength unto God: his excellency is over Israel, and his strength is in the clouds.
  1. (NIV) You are awesome, O God, in your sanctuary; the God of Israel gives power and strength to his people. Praise be to God!
  1. (KJV) O God, thou art terrible out of thy holy places: the God of Israel is he that giveth strength and power unto his people. Blessed be God.
  1. [4] Or prepare the way for him who rides through the deserts
  2. [6] Or the desolate in a homeland
  3. [13] Or saddlebags
  4. [14] Hebrew Shaddai
  5. [18] Or gifts for men, even
  6. [18] Or they
  7. [28] Many Hebrew manuscripts, Septuagint and Syriac; most Hebrew manuscripts Your God has summoned power for you
  8. [31] That is, the upper Nile region

Psalm 69

For the director of music. To [the tune of] "Lilies." Of David.
  1. (NIV) Save me, O God, for the waters have come up to my neck.
  1. (KJV) Save me, O God; for the waters are come in unto my soul.
  1. (NIV) I sink in the miry depths, where there is no foothold. I have come into the deep waters; the floods engulf me.
  1. (KJV) I sink in deep mire, where there is no standing: I am come into deep waters, where the floods overflow me.
  1. (NIV) I am worn out calling for help; my throat is parched. My eyes fail, looking for my God.
  1. (KJV) I am weary of my crying: my throat is dried: mine eyes fail while I wait for my God.
  1. (NIV) Those who hate me without reason outnumber the hairs of my head; many are my enemies without cause, those who seek to destroy me. I am forced to restore what I did not steal.
  1. (KJV) They that hate me without a cause are more than the hairs of mine head: they that would destroy me, being mine enemies wrongfully, are mighty: then I restored that which I took not away.
  1. (NIV) You know my folly, O God; my guilt is not hidden from you.
  1. (KJV) O God, thou knowest my foolishness; and my sins are not hid from thee.
  1. (NIV) May those who hope in you not be disgraced because of me, O Lord, the LORD Almighty; may those who seek you not be put to shame because of me, O God of Israel.
  1. (KJV) Let not them that wait on thee, O Lord GOD of hosts, be ashamed for my sake: let not those that seek thee be confounded for my sake, O God of Israel.
  1. (NIV) For I endure scorn for your sake, and shame covers my face.
  1. (KJV) Because for thy sake I have borne reproach; shame hath covered my face.
  1. (NIV) I am a stranger to my brothers, an alien to my own mother's sons;
  1. (KJV) I am become a stranger unto my brethren, and an alien unto my mother's children.
  1. (NIV) for zeal for your house consumes me, and the insults of those who insult you fall on me.
  1. (KJV) For the zeal of thine house hath eaten me up; and the reproaches of them that reproached thee are fallen upon me.
  1. (NIV) When I weep and fast, I must endure scorn;
  1. (KJV) When I wept, and chastened my soul with fasting, that was to my reproach.
  1. (NIV) when I put on sackcloth, people make sport of me.
  1. (KJV) I made sackcloth also my garment; and I became a proverb to them.
  1. (NIV) Those who sit at the gate mock me, and I am the song of the drunkards.
  1. (KJV) They that sit in the gate speak against me; and I was the song of the drunkards.
  1. (NIV) But I pray to you, O LORD, in the time of your favor; in your great love, O God, answer me with your sure salvation.
  1. (KJV) But as for me, my prayer is unto thee, O LORD, in an acceptable time: O God, in the multitude of thy mercy hear me, in the truth of thy salvation.
  1. (NIV) Rescue me from the mire, do not let me sink; deliver me from those who hate me, from the deep waters.
  1. (KJV) Deliver me out of the mire, and let me not sink: let me be delivered from them that hate me, and out of the deep waters.
  1. (NIV) Do not let the floodwaters engulf me or the depths swallow me up or the pit close its mouth over me.
  1. (KJV) Let not the waterflood overflow me, neither let the deep swallow me up, and let not the pit shut her mouth upon me.
  1. (NIV) Answer me, O LORD, out of the goodness of your love; in your great mercy turn to me.
  1. (KJV) Hear me, O LORD; for thy lovingkindness is good: turn unto me according to the multitude of thy tender mercies.
  1. (NIV) Do not hide your face from your servant; answer me quickly, for I am in trouble.
  1. (KJV) And hide not thy face from thy servant; for I am in trouble: hear me speedily.
  1. (NIV) Come near and rescue me; redeem me because of my foes.
  1. (KJV) Draw nigh unto my soul, and redeem it: deliver me because of mine enemies.
  1. (NIV) You know how I am scorned, disgraced and shamed; all my enemies are before you.
  1. (KJV) Thou hast known my reproach, and my shame, and my dishonour: mine adversaries are all before thee.
  1. (NIV) Scorn has broken my heart and has left me helpless; I looked for sympathy, but there was none, for comforters, but I found none.
  1. (KJV) Reproach hath broken my heart; and I am full of heaviness: and I looked for some to take pity, but there was none; and for comforters, but I found none.
  1. (NIV) They put gall in my food and gave me vinegar for my thirst.
  1. (KJV) They gave me also gall for my meat; and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.
  1. (NIV) May the table set before them become a snare; may it become retribution and [1] a trap.
  1. (KJV) Let their table become a snare before them: and that which should have been for their welfare, let it become a trap.
  1. (NIV) May their eyes be darkened so they cannot see, and their backs be bent forever.
  1. (KJV) Let their eyes be darkened, that they see not; and make their loins continually to shake.
  1. (NIV) Pour out your wrath on them; let your fierce anger overtake them.
  1. (KJV) Pour out thine indignation upon them, and let thy wrathful anger take hold of them.
  1. (NIV) May their place be deserted; let there be no one to dwell in their tents.
  1. (KJV) Let their habitation be desolate; and let none dwell in their tents.
  1. (NIV) For they persecute those you wound and talk about the pain of those you hurt.
  1. (KJV) For they persecute him whom thou hast smitten; and they talk to the grief of those whom thou hast wounded.
  1. (NIV) Charge them with crime upon crime; do not let them share in your salvation.
  1. (KJV) Add iniquity unto their iniquity: and let them not come into thy righteousness.
  1. (NIV) May they be blotted out of the book of life and not be listed with the righteous.
  1. (KJV) Let them be blotted out of the book of the living, and not be written with the righteous.
  1. (NIV) I am in pain and distress; may your salvation, O God, protect me.
  1. (KJV) But I am poor and sorrowful: let thy salvation, O God, set me up on high.
  1. (NIV) I will praise God's name in song and glorify him with thanksgiving.
  1. (KJV) I will praise the name of God with a song, and will magnify him with thanksgiving.
  1. (NIV) This will please the LORD more than an ox, more than a bull with its horns and hoofs.
  1. (KJV) This also shall please the LORD better than an ox or bullock that hath horns and hoofs.
  1. (NIV) The poor will see and be glad-- you who seek God, may your hearts live!
  1. (KJV) The humble shall see this, and be glad: and your heart shall live that seek God.
  1. (NIV) The LORD hears the needy and does not despise his captive people.
  1. (KJV) For the LORD heareth the poor, and despiseth not his prisoners.
  1. (NIV) Let heaven and earth praise him, the seas and all that move in them,
  1. (KJV) Let the heaven and earth praise him, the seas, and everything that moveth therein.
  1. (NIV) for God will save Zion and rebuild the cities of Judah. Then people will settle there and possess it;
  1. (KJV) For God will save Zion, and will build the cities of Judah: that they may dwell there, and have it in possession.
  1. (NIV) the children of his servants will inherit it, and those who love his name will dwell there.
  1. (KJV) The seed also of his servants shall inherit it: and they that love his name shall dwell therein.
  1. [22] Or snare and their fellowship become

Psalm 70

For the director of music. Of David. A petition.
  1. (NIV) Hasten, O God, to save me; O LORD, come quickly to help me.
  1. (KJV) Make haste, O God, to deliver me; make haste to help me, O LORD.
  1. (NIV) May those who seek my life be put to shame and confusion; may all who desire my ruin be turned back in disgrace.
  1. (KJV) Let them be ashamed and confounded that seek after my soul: let them be turned backward, and put to confusion, that desire my hurt.
  1. (NIV) May those who say to me, "Aha! Aha!" turn back because of their shame.
  1. (KJV) Let them be turned back for a reward of their shame that say, Aha, aha.
  1. (NIV) But may all who seek you rejoice and be glad in you; may those who love your salvation always say, "Let God be exalted!"
  1. (KJV) Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: and let such as love thy salvation say continually, Let God be magnified.
  1. (NIV) Yet I am poor and needy; come quickly to me, O God. You are my help and my deliverer; O LORD, do not delay.
  1. (KJV) But I am poor and needy: make haste unto me, O God: thou art my help and my deliverer; O LORD, make no tarrying.

Psalm 71

  1. (NIV) In you, O LORD, I have taken refuge; let me never be put to shame.
  1. (KJV) In thee, O LORD, do I put my trust: let me never be put to confusion.
  1. (NIV) Rescue me and deliver me in your righteousness; turn your ear to me and save me.
  1. (KJV) Deliver me in thy righteousness, and cause me to escape: incline thine ear unto me, and save me.
  1. (NIV) Be my rock of refuge, to which I can always go; give the command to save me, for you are my rock and my fortress.
  1. (KJV) Be thou my strong habitation, whereunto I may continually resort: thou hast given commandment to save me; for thou art my rock and my fortress.
  1. (NIV) Deliver me, O my God, from the hand of the wicked, from the grasp of evil and cruel men.
  1. (KJV) Deliver me, O my God, out of the hand of the wicked, out of the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.
  1. (NIV) For you have been my hope, O Sovereign LORD, my confidence since my youth.
  1. (KJV) For thou art my hope, O Lord GOD: thou art my trust from my youth.
  1. (NIV) From birth I have relied on you; you brought me forth from my mother's womb. I will ever praise you.
  1. (KJV) By thee have I been holden up from the womb: thou art he that took me out of my mother's bowels: my praise shall be continually of thee.
  1. (NIV) I have become like a portent to many, but you are my strong refuge.
  1. (KJV) I am as a wonder unto many; but thou art my strong refuge.
  1. (NIV) My mouth is filled with your praise, declaring your splendor all day long.
  1. (KJV) Let my mouth be filled with thy praise and with thy honour all the day.
  1. (NIV) Do not cast me away when I am old; do not forsake me when my strength is gone.
  1. (KJV) Cast me not off in the time of old age; forsake me not when my strength faileth.
  1. (NIV) For my enemies speak against me; those who wait to kill me conspire together.
  1. (KJV) For mine enemies speak against me; and they that lay wait for my soul take counsel together,
  1. (NIV) They say, "God has forsaken him; pursue him and seize him, for no one will rescue him."
  1. (KJV) Saying, God hath forsaken him: persecute and take him; for there is none to deliver him.
  1. (NIV) Be not far from me, O God; come quickly, O my God, to help me.
  1. (KJV) O God, be not far from me: O my God, make haste for my help.
  1. (NIV) May my accusers perish in shame; may those who want to harm me be covered with scorn and disgrace.
  1. (KJV) Let them be confounded and consumed that are adversaries to my soul; let them be covered with reproach and dishonour that seek my hurt.
  1. (NIV) But as for me, I will always have hope; I will praise you more and more.
  1. (KJV) But I will hope continually, and will yet praise thee more and more.
  1. (NIV) My mouth will tell of your righteousness, of your salvation all day long, though I know not its measure.
  1. (KJV) My mouth shall shew forth thy righteousness and thy salvation all the day; for I know not the numbers thereof.
  1. (NIV) I will come and proclaim your mighty acts, O Sovereign LORD; I will proclaim your righteousness, yours alone.
  1. (KJV) I will go in the strength of the Lord GOD: I will make mention of thy righteousness, even of thine only.
  1. (NIV) Since my youth, O God, you have taught me, and to this day I declare your marvelous deeds.
  1. (KJV) O God, thou hast taught me from my youth: and hitherto have I declared thy wondrous works.
  1. (NIV) Even when I am old and gray, do not forsake me, O God, till I declare your power to the next generation, your might to all who are to come.
  1. (KJV) Now also when I am old and grayheaded, O God, forsake me not; until I have shewed thy strength unto this generation, and thy power to every one that is to come.
  1. (NIV) Your righteousness reaches to the skies, O God, you who have done great things. Who, O God, is like you?
  1. (KJV) Thy righteousness also, O God, is very high, who hast done great things: O God, who is like unto thee!
  1. (NIV) Though you have made me see troubles, many and bitter, you will restore my life again; from the depths of the earth you will again bring me up.
  1. (KJV) Thou, which hast shewed me great and sore troubles, shalt quicken me again, and shalt bring me up again from the depths of the earth.
  1. (NIV) You will increase my honor and comfort me once again.
  1. (KJV) Thou shalt increase my greatness, and comfort me on every side.
  1. (NIV) I will praise you with the harp for your faithfulness, O my God; I will sing praise to you with the lyre, O Holy One of Israel.
  1. (KJV) I will also praise thee with the psaltery, even thy truth, O my God: unto thee will I sing with the harp, O thou Holy One of Israel.
  1. (NIV) My lips will shout for joy when I sing praise to you-- I, whom you have redeemed.
  1. (KJV) My lips shall greatly rejoice when I sing unto thee; and my soul, which thou hast redeemed.
  1. (NIV) My tongue will tell of your righteous acts all day long, for those who wanted to harm me have been put to shame and confusion.
  1. (KJV) My tongue also shall talk of thy righteousness all the day long: for they are confounded, for they are brought unto shame, that seek my hurt.

Psalm 72

Of Solomon.
  1. (NIV) Endow the king with your justice, O God, the royal son with your righteousness.
  1. (KJV) Give the king thy judgments, O God, and thy righteousness unto the king's son.
  1. (NIV) He will [1] judge your people in righteousness, your afflicted ones with justice.
  1. (KJV) He shall judge thy people with righteousness, and thy poor with judgment.
  1. (NIV) The mountains will bring prosperity to the people, the hills the fruit of righteousness.
  1. (KJV) The mountains shall bring peace to the people, and the little hills, by righteousness.
  1. (NIV) He will defend the afflicted among the people and save the children of the needy; he will crush the oppressor.
  1. (KJV) He shall judge the poor of the people, he shall save the children of the needy, and shall break in pieces the oppressor.
  1. (NIV) He will endure [2] as long as the sun, as long as the moon, through all generations.
  1. (KJV) They shall fear thee as long as the sun and moon endure, throughout all generations.
  1. (NIV) He will be like rain falling on a mown field, like showers watering the earth.
  1. (KJV) He shall come down like rain upon the mown grass: as showers that water the earth.
  1. (NIV) In his days the righteous will flourish; prosperity will abound till the moon is no more.
  1. (KJV) In his days shall the righteous flourish; and abundance of peace so long as the moon endureth.
  1. (NIV) He will rule from sea to sea and from the River [3] to the ends of the earth. [4]
  1. (KJV) He shall have dominion also from sea to sea, and from the river unto the ends of the earth.
  1. (NIV) The desert tribes will bow before him and his enemies will lick the dust.
  1. (KJV) They that dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him; and his enemies shall lick the dust.
  1. (NIV) The kings of Tarshish and of distant shores will bring tribute to him; the kings of Sheba and Seba will present him gifts.
  1. (KJV) The kings of Tarshish and of the isles shall bring presents: the kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.
  1. (NIV) All kings will bow down to him and all nations will serve him.
  1. (KJV) Yea, all kings shall fall down before him: all nations shall serve him.
  1. (NIV) For he will deliver the needy who cry out, the afflicted who have no one to help.
  1. (KJV) For he shall deliver the needy when he crieth; the poor also, and him that hath no helper.
  1. (NIV) He will take pity on the weak and the needy and save the needy from death.
  1. (KJV) He shall spare the poor and needy, and shall save the souls of the needy.
  1. (NIV) He will rescue them from oppression and violence, for precious is their blood in his sight.
  1. (KJV) He shall redeem their soul from deceit and violence: and precious shall their blood be in his sight.
  1. (NIV) Long may he live! May gold from Sheba be given him. May people ever pray for him and bless him all day long.
  1. (KJV) And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Sheba: prayer also shall be made for him continually; and daily shall he be praised.

Psalm 102

A prayer of an afflicted man. When he is faint and pours out his lament before the LORD.
  1. (NIV) Hear my prayer, O LORD; let my cry for help come to you.
  1. (KJV) Hear my prayer, O LORD, and let my cry come unto thee.
  1. (NIV) Do not hide your face from me when I am in distress. Turn your ear to me; when I call, answer me quickly.
  1. (KJV) Hide not thy face from me in the day when I am in trouble; incline thine ear unto me: in the day when I call answer me speedily.
  1. (NIV) For my days vanish like smoke; my bones burn like glowing embers.
  1. (KJV) For my days are consumed like smoke, and my bones are burned as an hearth.
  1. (NIV) My heart is blighted and withered like grass; I forget to eat my food.

Psalm 120

A song of ascents.
  1. (NIV) I call on the LORD in my distress, and he answers me.
  1. (KJV) In my distress I cried unto the LORD, and he heard me.
  1. (NIV) Save me, O LORD, from lying lips and from deceitful tongues.
  1. (KJV) Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips, and from a deceitful tongue.
  1. (NIV) What will he do to you, and what more besides, O deceitful tongue?
  1. (KJV) What shall be given unto thee? or what shall be done unto thee, thou false tongue?
  1. (NIV) He will punish you with a warrior's sharp arrows, with burning coals of the broom tree.
  1. (KJV) Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper.
  1. (NIV) Woe to me that I dwell in Meshech, that I live among the tents of Kedar!
  1. (KJV) Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, that I dwell in the tents of Kedar!
  1. (NIV) Too long have I lived among those who hate peace.
  1. (KJV) My soul hath long dwelt with him that hateth peace.
  1. (NIV) I am a man of peace; but when I speak, they are for war.
  1. (KJV) I am for peace: but when I speak, they are for war.

Psalm 121

A song of ascents.
  1. (NIV) I lift up my eyes to the hills-- where does my help come from?
  1. (KJV) I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.
  1. (NIV) My help comes from the LORD, the Maker of heaven and earth.
  1. (KJV) My help cometh from the LORD, which made heaven and earth.
  1. (NIV) He will not let your foot slip-- he who watches over you will not slumber;
  1. (KJV) He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber.
  1. (NIV) indeed, he who watches over Israel will neither slumber nor sleep.
  1. (KJV) Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep.
  1. (NIV) The LORD watches over you-- the LORD is your shade at your right hand;
  1. (KJV) The LORD is thy keeper: the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.
  1. (NIV) the sun will not harm you by day, nor the moon by night.
  1. (KJV) The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night.
  1. (NIV) The LORD will keep you from all harm-- he will watch over your life;

Psalm 145

A psalm of praise. Of David. [1]
  1. (NIV) I will exalt you, my God the King; I will praise your name for ever and ever.
  1. (KJV) I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for ever and ever.
  1. (NIV) Every day I will praise you and extol your name for ever and ever.
  1. (KJV) Every day will I bless thee; and I will praise thy name for ever and ever.
  1. (NIV) Great is the LORD and most worthy of praise; his greatness no one can fathom.
  1. (KJV) Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised; and his greatness is unsearchable.
  1. (NIV) One generation will commend your works to another; they will tell of your mighty acts.
  1. (KJV) One generation shall praise thy works to another, and shall declare thy mighty acts.
  1. (NIV) They will speak of the glorious splendor of your majesty, and I will meditate on your wonderful works. [2]
  1. (KJV) I will speak of the glorious honour of thy majesty, and of thy wondrous works.
  1. (NIV) They will tell of the power of your awesome works, and I will proclaim your great deeds.
  1. (KJV) And men shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and I will declare thy greatness.
  1. (NIV) They will celebrate your abundant goodness and joyfully sing of your righteousness.
  1. (KJV) They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness, and shall sing of thy righteousness.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is gracious and compassionate, slow to anger and rich in love.
  1. (KJV) The LORD is gracious, and full of compassion; slow to anger, and of great mercy.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is good to all; he has compassion on all he has made.
  1. (KJV) The LORD is good to all: and his tender mercies are over all his works.
  1. (NIV) All you have made will praise you, O LORD; your saints will extol you.
  1. (KJV) All thy works shall praise thee, O LORD; and thy saints shall bless thee.
  1. (NIV) They will tell of the glory of your kingdom and speak of your might,
  1. (KJV) They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, and talk of thy power;
  1. (NIV) so that all men may know of your mighty acts and the glorious splendor of your kingdom.
  1. (KJV) To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, and the glorious majesty of his kingdom.
  1. (NIV) Your kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and your dominion endures through all generations. The LORD is faithful to all his promises and loving toward all he has made. [3]
  1. (KJV) Thy kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and thy dominion endureth throughout all generations.
  1. (NIV) The LORD upholds all those who fall and lifts up all who are bowed down.
  1. (KJV) The LORD upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all those that be bowed down.
  1. (NIV) The eyes of all look to you, and you give them their food at the proper time.
  1. (KJV) The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them their meat in due season.
  1. (NIV) You open your hand and satisfy the desires of every living thing.
  1. (KJV) Thou openest thine hand, and satisfiest the desire of every living thing.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is righteous in all his ways and loving toward all he has made.
  1. (KJV) The LORD is righteous in all his ways, and holy in all his works.
  1. (NIV) The LORD is near to all who call on him, to all who call on him in truth.
  1. (KJV) The LORD is nigh unto all them that call upon him, to all that call upon him in truth.
  1. (NIV) He fulfills the desires of those who fear him; he hears their cry and saves them.
  1. (KJV) He will fulfil the desire of them that fear him: he also will hear their cry, and will save them.
  1. (NIV) The LORD watches over all who love him, but all the wicked he will destroy.
  1. (KJV) The LORD preserveth all them that love him: but all the wicked will he destroy.
  1. (NIV) My mouth will speak in praise of the LORD. Let every creature praise his holy name for ever and ever.
  1. (KJV) My mouth shall speak the praise of the LORD: and let all flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever.
  1. [Title] This psalm is an acrostic poem, the verses of which (including verse 13b) begin with the successive letters of the Hebrew alphabet.
  2. [5] Dead Sea Scrolls and Syriac (see also Septuagint); Masoretic Text On the glorious splendor of your majesty and on your wonderful works I will meditate
  3. [13] One manuscript of the Masoretic Text, Dead Sea Scrolls and Syriac (see also Septuagint); most manuscripts of the Masoretic Text do not have the last two lines of verse 13.

  1. (NIV) I will praise the LORD all my life; I will sing praise to my God as long as I live.
  1. (KJV) While I live will I praise the LORD: I will sing praises unto my God while I have any being.
  1. (NIV) Do not put your trust in princes, in mortal men, who cannot save.
  1. (KJV) Put not your trust in princes, nor in the son of man, in whom there is no help.
  1. (NIV) When their spirit departs, they return to the ground; on that very day their plans come to nothing.
  1. (KJV) His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that very day his thoughts perish.
  1. (NIV) Blessed is he whose help is the God of Jacob, whose hope is in the LORD his God,
  1. (KJV) Happy is he that hath the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope is in the LORD his God:
  1. (NIV) the Maker of heaven and earth, the sea, and everything in them-- the LORD, who remains faithful forever.
  1. (KJV) Which made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that therein is: which keepeth truth for ever:
  1. (NIV) He upholds the cause of the oppressed and gives food to the hungry. The LORD sets prisoners free,
  1. (KJV) Which executeth judgment for the oppressed: which giveth food to the hungry. The LORD looseth the prisoners:
  1. (NIV) the LORD gives sight to the blind, the LORD lifts up those who are bowed down, the LORD loves the righteous.
  1. (KJV) The LORD openeth the eyes of the blind: the LORD raiseth them that are bowed down: the LORD loveth the righteous:
  1. (NIV) The LORD watches over the alien and sustains the fatherless and the widow, but he frustrates the ways of the wicked.
  1. (KJV) The LORD preserveth the strangers; he relieveth the fatherless and widow: but the way of the wicked he turneth upside down.
  1. (NIV) The LORD reigns forever, your God, O Zion, for all generations. Praise the LORD.
  1. (KJV) The LORD shall reign for ever, even thy God, O Zion, unto all generations. Praise ye the LORD.
  1. [1] Hebrew Hallelu Yah; also in verse 10

Psalm 147

  1. (NIV) Praise the LORD. [1] How good it is to sing praises to our God, how pleasant and fitting to praise him!
  1. (KJV) Praise ye the LORD: for it is good to sing praises unto our God; for it is pleasant; and praise is comely.
  1. (NIV) The LORD builds up Jerusalem; he gathers the exiles of Israel.
  1. (KJV) The LORD doth build up Jerusalem: he gathereth together the outcasts of Israel.
  1. (NIV) He heals the brokenhearted and binds up their wounds.
  1. (KJV) He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their wounds.
  1. (NIV) He determines the number of the stars and calls them each by name.
  1. (KJV) He telleth the number of the stars; he calleth them all by their names.
  1. (NIV) Great is our Lord and mighty in power; his understanding has no limit.
  1. (KJV) Great is our Lord, and of great power: his understanding is infinite.
  1. (NIV) The LORD sustains the humble but casts the wicked to the ground.
  1. (KJV) The LORD lifteth up the meek: he casteth the wicked down to the ground.
  1. (NIV) Sing to the LORD with thanksgiving; make music to our God on the harp.
  1. (KJV) Sing unto the LORD with thanksgiving; sing praise upon the harp unto our God:
  1. (NIV) He covers the sky with clouds; he supplies the earth with rain and makes grass grow on the hills.
  1. (KJV) Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains.
  1. (NIV) He provides food for the cattle and for the young ravens when they call.
  1. (KJV) He giveth to the beast his food, and to the young ravens which cry.
  1. (NIV) His pleasure is not in the strength of the horse, nor his delight in the legs of a man;
  1. (KJV) He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: he taketh not pleasure in the legs of a man.
  1. (NIV) the LORD delights in those who fear him, who put their hope in his unfailing love.
  1. (KJV) The LORD taketh pleasure in them that fear him, in those that hope in his mercy.
  1. (NIV) Extol the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise your God, O Zion,
  1. (KJV) Praise the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion.
  1. (NIV) for he strengthens the bars of your gates and blesses your people within you.
  1. (KJV) For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath blessed thy children within thee.
  1. (NIV) He grants peace to your borders and satisfies you with the finest of wheat.
  1. (KJV) He maketh peace in thy borders, and filleth thee with the finest of the wheat.
  1. (NIV) He sends his command to the earth; his word runs swiftly.
  1. (KJV) He sendeth forth his commandment upon earth: his word runneth very swiftly.
  1. (NIV) He spreads the snow like wool and scatters the frost like ashes.
  1. (KJV) He giveth snow like wool: he scattereth the hoarfrost like ashes.
  1. (NIV) He hurls down his hail like pebbles. Who can withstand his icy blast?
  1. (KJV) He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand before his cold?
  1. (NIV) He sends his word and melts them; he stirs up his breezes, and the waters flow.
  1. (KJV) He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: he causeth his wind to blow, and the waters flow.
  1. (NIV) He has revealed his word to Jacob, his laws and decrees to Israel.
  1. (KJV) He sheweth his word unto Jacob, his statutes and his judgments unto Israel.
  1. (NIV) He has done this for no other nation; they do not know his laws. Praise the LORD.
  1. (KJV) He hath not dealt so with any nation: and as for his judgments, they have not known them. Praise ye the LORD.
  1. [1] Hebrew Hallelu Yah; also in verse 20

Psalm 148

  1. (NIV) Praise the LORD. [1] Praise the LORD from the heavens, praise him in the heights above.
  1. (KJV) Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the LORD from the heavens: praise him in the heights.
  1. (NIV) Praise him, all his angels, praise him, all his heavenly hosts.
  1. (KJV) Praise ye him, all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts.
  1. (NIV) Praise him, sun and moon, praise him, all you shining stars.
  1. (KJV) Praise ye him, sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars of light.
  1. (NIV) Praise him, you highest heavens and you waters above the skies.
  1. (KJV) Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that be above the heavens.
  1. (NIV) Let them praise the name of the LORD, for he commanded and they were created.
  1. (KJV) Let them praise the name of the LORD: for he commanded, and they were created.
  1. (NIV) He set them in place for ever and ever; he gave a decree that will never pass away.
  1. (KJV) He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: he hath made a decree which shall not pass.
  1. (NIV) Praise the LORD from the earth, you great sea creatures and all ocean depths,
  1. (KJV) Praise the LORD from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps:
  1. (NIV) lightning and hail, snow and clouds, stormy winds that do his bidding,
  1. (KJV) Fire, and hail; snow, and vapour; stormy wind fulfilling his word:
  1. (NIV) you mountains and all hills, fruit trees and all cedars,
  1. (KJV) Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars:
  1. (NIV) wild animals and all cattle, small creatures and flying birds,
  1. (KJV) Beasts, and all cattle; creeping things, and flying fowl:
  1. (NIV) kings of the earth and all nations, you princes and all rulers on earth,
  1. (KJV) Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of the earth:
  1. (NIV) young men and maidens, old men and children.
  1. (KJV) Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children:
  1. (NIV) Let them praise the name of the LORD, for his name alone is exalted; his splendor is above the earth and the heavens.
  1. (KJV) Let them praise the name of the LORD: for his name alone is excellent; his glory is above the earth and heaven.
  1. (NIV) He has raised up for his people a horn, [2] the praise of all his saints, of Israel, the people close to his heart. Praise the LORD.
  1. (KJV) He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints; even of the children of Israel, a people near unto him. Praise ye the LORD.
  1. [1] Hebrew Hallelu Yah; also in verse 14
  2. [14] Horn here symbolizes strong one, that is, king.

Psalm 149

  1. (NIV) Praise the LORD. [1] Sing to the LORD a new song, his praise in the assembly of the saints.
  1. (KJV) Praise ye the LORD. Sing unto the LORD a new song, and his praise in the congregation of saints.
  1. (NIV) Let Israel rejoice in their Maker; let the people of Zion be glad in their King.
  1. (KJV) Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.
  1. (NIV) Let them praise his name with dancing and make music to him with tambourine and harp.
  1. (KJV) Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises unto him with the timbrel and harp.
  1. (NIV) For the LORD takes delight in his people; he crowns the humble with salvation.
  1. (KJV) For the LORD taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the meek with salvation.
  1. (NIV) Let the saints rejoice in this honor and sing for joy on their beds.
  1. (KJV) Let the saints be joyful in glory: let them sing aloud upon their beds.
  1. (NIV) May the praise of God be in their mouths and a double-edged sword in their hands,
  1. (KJV) Let the high praises of God be in their mouth, and a twoedged sword in their hand;
  1. (NIV) to inflict vengeance on the nations and punishment on the peoples,
  1. (KJV) To execute vengeance upon the heathen, and punishments upon the people;
  1. (NIV) to bind their kings with fetters, their nobles with shackles of iron,
  1. (KJV) To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters of iron;
  1. (NIV) to carry out the sentence written against them. This is the glory of all his saints. Praise the LORD.
  1. (KJV) To execute upon them the judgment written: this honour have all his saints. Praise ye the LORD.
  1. [1] Hebrew Hallelu Yah; also in verse 9

Psalm 150

  1. (NIV) Praise the LORD. [1] Praise God in his sanctuary; praise him in his mighty heavens.
  1. (KJV) Praise ye the LORD. Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in the firmament of his power.
  1. (NIV) Praise him for his acts of power; praise him for his surpassing greatness.
  1. (KJV) Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his excellent greatness.
  1. (NIV) Praise him with the sounding of the trumpet, praise him with the harp and lyre,
  1. (KJV) Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the psaltery and harp.
  1. (NIV) praise him with tambourine and dancing, praise him with the strings and flute,
  1. (KJV) Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed instruments and organs.
  1. (NIV) praise him with the clash of cymbals, praise him with resounding cymbals.
  1. (KJV) Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high sounding cymbals.
  1. (NIV) Let everything that has breath praise the LORD. Praise the LORD.
  1. (KJV) Let every thing that hath breath praise the LORD. Praise ye the LORD.
  1. [1] Hebrew Hallelu Yah; also in verse 6
